<h2 class="wp-block-heading alignwide is-style-section_ttl u-mb-ctrl u-mb-10 has-swl-main-color has-text-color">配布場所マップ</h2>



<div class="swell-block-fullWide pc-py-0 sp-py-0 alignfull"><div class="swell-block-fullWide__inner l-container"><div class="p-postListWrap u-mb-ctrl u-mb-0 -pc-col6"><ul class="p-postList -type-card -pc-col3 -sp-col2"><li class="p-postList__item">
	<a href="https://anythingsearch.info/map/" class="p-postList__link">
		<div class="p-postList__thumb c-postThumb">
	<figure class="c-postThumb__figure">
		<img decoding="async" width="1024" height="1024"  src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" alt="" class="c-postThumb__img u-obf-cover lazyload" sizes="(min-width: 960px) 400px, 50vw" data-src="https://anythingsearch.info/card/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/MAP3-1024x1024.png" data-srcset="https://anythingsearch.info/card/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/MAP3-1024x1024.png 1024w, https://anythingsearch.info/card/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/MAP3-300x300.png 300w, https://anythingsearch.info/card/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/MAP3-150x150.png 150w, https://anythingsearch.info/card/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/MAP3-768x768.png 768w, https://anythingsearch.info/card/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/MAP3-1536x1536.png 1536w, https://anythingsearch.info/card/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/MAP3.png 1571w" data-aspectratio="1024/1024" ><noscript><img decoding="async" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" data-src="https://anythingsearch.info/card/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/MAP3-1024x1024.png" class="c-postThumb__img u-obf-cover lazyload" alt="" width="1024" data-aspectratio="1024/1024"><noscript><img decoding="async" src="https://anythingsearch.info/card/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/MAP3-1024x1024.png" class="c-postThumb__img u-obf-cover" alt=""></noscript></noscript>	</figure>
	</div>
					<div class="p-postList__body">
				<h2 class="p-postList__title">マンホールカード配布場所マップ</h2>									<div class="p-postList__excerpt">
						このマップは、マンホールカードの配布場所を表示しています。<br>マップ上のカード画像をクリックすると配布場所の情報が表示されます。<br>「ルートを表示」ボタンを押すと現在地から配布場所までのルートがGoogleMapsで表示されます。<br>「蓋を見に行く」ボタンを押すと現在地から蓋の設置場所(カードに表示の座標)までのルートがGoogleMapsで表示されます。					</div>
								<div class="p-postList__meta">
									</div>
			</div>
			</a>
</li>
<li class="p-postList__item">
	<a href="https://anythingsearch.info/pokemon/pokemon-manhole-map/" class="p-postList__link">
		<div class="p-postList__thumb c-postThumb">
	<figure class="c-postThumb__figure">

(function () {
	const timeout = 3000;
	const loadTimer = timeout ? setTimeout(loadJs,timeout) : null;
	const userEvents = ["mouseover","keydown","wheel","touchmove touchend","touchstart touchend"];
	userEvents.forEach(function(e){
		window.addEventListener(e,eTrigger,{passive:!0})
	});
	function eTrigger(){
		loadJs();
		if(null !== loadTimer) clearTimeout(loadTimer);
		userEvents.forEach(function(e){
			window.removeEventListener(e,eTrigger,{passive:!0});
		});
	}
	function loadJs(){
		document.querySelectorAll("script[data-swldelayedjs]").forEach(function(el){
			el.setAttribute("src",el.getAttribute("data-swldelayedjs"));
		});
	}
})();
</script>
